        <h1 class="se-t sie-hero_7-text st-m-title st-d-title se-rc">
         Welcome
        </h1>
       </div>
       <div class="sie-hero_8 se " data-sid="hero_8">

We partner with each client to provide expert project management and personalized designs from start to finish. We specialize in giving each client impeccable attention to detail and turning ideas into reality.

         Yingka Chou

       <a class="sie-about_yingka_4 se se-sl se-stl" data-sid="about_yingka_4" data-state="about|0|0|0" href="#about" target="_self">

          </path>

       <div class="sie-about_yingka_6 se " data-sid="about_yingka_6">
        <p class="se-t sie-about_yingka_6-text st-m-paragraph st-d-paragraph se-rc">
         Yingka brings over a decade of professional experience of producing and coordinating over 700 distinctive events and weddings personally designed and managed. She thrives under stressful situations with grace and patience as these skills were further enhanced when she graduated from USC with a BA in Interpersonal Communications and Business Organization. In addition to being an impeccable and obsessively organized coordinator, her passion for flowers led her to become a floral and event designer thus establishing Master Plans Events &amp; Designs as a full-service company since 2009. Her list of events and designs include high end weddings, galas, gift lounges and charity events.
        </p>

        </div>

       <div class="sie-about_taylor_3 se " data-sid="about_taylor_3">
        <h1 class="se-t sie-about_taylor_3-text st-m-title st-d-title se-rc">
         Taylor Hall
        </h1>
       </div>
       <a class="sie-about_taylor_4 se se-sl se-stl" data-sid="about_taylor_4" data-state="about|0|0|0" href="#about" target="_self">
        <div class="se-icon">
         <svg viewbox="0 0 512 512" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">
          <path d="M405 136.798L375.202 107 256 226.202 136.798 107 107 136.798 226.202 256 107 375.202 136.798 405 256 285.798 375.202 405 405 375.202 285.798 256">
          </path>
         </svg>
        </div>
       </a>
       <a class="sie-about_taylor_5 se se-sl se-stl" data-sid="about_taylor_5" data-state="about|next|0|0" href="#about" target="_self">
        <div class="se-icon">
         <svg viewbox="0 0 512 512" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">
          <path d="M85 277.375h259.704L225.002 397.077 256 427l171-171L256 85l-29.922 29.924 118.626 119.701H85v42.75z">
          </path>
         </svg>
        </div>
       </a>
       <div class="sie-about_taylor_6 se " data-sid="about_taylor_6">
        <p class="se-t sie-about_taylor_6-text st-m-paragraph st-d-paragraph se-rc">
         Taylor recently joined Master Plans Events and is an integral part in making each event seamless. Having graduated from the University of California, Santa Barbara, where she earned her Bachelor’s Degree in Communication, it is there that she found her passion for event planning, working for two nonprofit organizations assisting in planning their annual fundraising events. During her time at the nonprofit organization, Taylor developed a passion for creating lavish galas while serving her community. She was able to excel and thrive in this environment with her keen eye for detail and her amazing organizational skills. Since working with Master Plans Events, Taylor has had the opportunity to immerse herself in the wedding industry along with continuing to assist with nonprofit events.
        </p>
       </div>
       <div class="sie-about_taylor_7 se " data-sid="about_taylor_7">

         Assistant Studio Coordinator
        </h3>
       </div>

        <h1 class="se-t sie-about_quynh-anh_3-text st-m-title st-d-title se-rc">
         Quynh Anh Tran
        </h1>
       </div>
       <a class="sie-about_quynh-anh_4 se se-sl se-stl" data-sid="about_quynh-anh_4" data-state="about|0|0|0" href="#about" target="_self">
        <div class="se-icon">
         <svg viewbox="0 0 512 512" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">
          <path d="M405 136.798L375.202 107 256 226.202 136.798 107 107 136.798 226.202 256 107 375.202 136.798 405 256 285.798 375.202 405 405 375.202 285.798 256">
          </path>
         </svg>
        </div>
       </a>
       <a class="sie-about_quynh-anh_5 se se-sl se-stl" data-sid="about_quynh-anh_5" data-state="about|1|0|0" href="#about" target="_self">
        <div class="se-icon">
         <svg viewbox="0 0 512 512" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">
          <path d="M85 277.375h259.704L225.002 397.077 256 427l171-171L256 85l-29.922 29.924 118.626 119.701H85v42.75z">
          </path>
         </svg>
        </div>
       </a>
       <div class="sie-about_quynh-anh_6 se " data-sid="about_quynh-anh_6">
        <p class="se-t sie-about_quynh-anh_6-text st-m-paragraph st-d-paragraph se-rc">
         A San Francisco Bay Area native, Quynh Anh (pronounced “Quinn-Un”) is no stranger to planning events. From helping her mother execute family parties at a young age to organizing events for her fraternity at UC Davis, she decided early on that she was determined to become a Wedding Coordinator! Quynh Anh took her first professional steps into the wedding industry in 2015 learning under the Association of Certified Professional Wedding Consultants and continually applies this knowledge everyday while doing what she loves! Quynh Anh loves to celebrate and embrace different cultures and has a B.A. in Asian American Studies with a minor in Anthropology.
        </p>
